THE KARMAPA

*, ,DA LAM BDAG CAG RNAMS KYI YONGS 'DZIN DGE BA'I BSHES GNYEN
MKHAN

CHEN KHRA 'GU RIN PO CHE'I THUGS BSKYED DANG MDZAD BZANG GI LEGS
SPYAD LAS NYE BAR 'ONG

BA'I \BADZRA BIDY'A GSUNG RAB DPE BSKRUN KHANG\ ZHES GSAR DU DBU
BRNYES PA 'DI NYID

BRGYUD GANGS CAN GYI LJONGS 'DIR GNA' BO'I DUS NAS MA NYAMS PA'I
RMAD BYUNG GTZUG

PA'I MKHAS GRUB GONG MA DAG GI GSUNG RAB RGYA CHEN ZAB MO'I DPAL
YON GYIS PHYUG PA

KUN KYANG SNGAR RJES SHUL 'DZIN DANG, PHYI RJES DAR SPEL GYI SGO
NAS PHAN BDE'I 'BYUNG

GNAS RGYAL BA'I BSTAN PA RIN PO CHE'I NGES DON LUNG RTOGS KYI
CHOS TSUL 'CHAD NYAN SGOM

GSUM GYI GNAS GANG CIR ZHABS 'DEGS SU 'GRO BA'I YID SMON RNAM
DAG BCAS

RNAM GROL BGROD PA'I LAM GCIG PU, ,

LUNG RTOGS GNYIS BSDUS ZHI BSIL CHOS, ,

GUS PA'I PHYAG GI YUL DU BSTEN, ,

DE YANG GANGS CAN BOD KYI LJONGS SU SANGS RGYAS KYI BSTAN PA DAR
BA NAS BRTZAMS DA?

LTA'I BAR DU, MKHAS BTZUN BZANG GRUB KYI SKYES BU KHYAD PAR CAN
BSAM GYIS MI KHYAB

PA ZHIG BYON PA RNAMS KYIS, RANG RANG GI NYAMS MYONG GIS STENG
NAS BYUNG BA'I MAN NGAG

SNA TSOGS PA ZHIG ,MA 'ONGS PA'I MI RABS RIM 'BYUNG RNAMS LA
THUGS BRTZE BA CHEN

POS NYE BAR DGONGS TE, BSTAN BCOS DANG, ZHAL GDAMS, ZIN BRIS
DANG, CHO GA

LO RGYUS DANG, RNAM THAR SOGS, BSAM GYIS MI KHYAB PA ZHIG RTZOM
BRIS GNANG STE

BZHUGS PA DE DAG BAR LAM DUS KYI 'GYUR BA LA BRTEN NAS MANG PO
ZHIG CHUD ZOS

SU PHYIN PA NI BOD PHYI NANG TZAM MA YIN PAR, 'DZAM GLING GI
SKYE 'GRO YONGS LA GYONG GUN

CHEN PO ZHIG BYUNG STE, SHIN TU PHANGS PA'I GNAS SU GYUR PAR MA
ZAD, DA LTA 'GRO BA'I

BSOD NAMS KYI SKAL PAR BZHUGS PA DAG LAS KYANG, KHA SHAS DPE
RGYUN DKON PAS

MI MNGON PA'I DBYINGS SU PHEBS LA NYE BA RNAMS MI NYAMS PAR DPE
RGYUN SPEL BA'I

CHED DANG, YANG PHYAG DPE SHIN TU MKHO GAL CHE BA KHAG THOS BSAM
DANG, NYAMS

LEN GNANG MKHAN, DPAL 'BYOR GYI RGYAB RTEN DE TZAM MED PAR, SPRO
MED DU BZHUGS

GYUR THUGS MNYES PA RNAMS KYIS STABS BDE'I THOG NAS PHYAG DPE
KHAG THOB PA'I

CHED, BADZRA BIDY'A'I DPE MDZOD KHANG GIS PAR SKRUN ZHUS DANG
ZHU 'CHAR BZHIN, DA LAM

SBYIN PA'I BDAG PO BLA MA BSOD NAMS DBANG PHYUG DANG KARMA ZLA
BA RNAM GNYIS NAS

ZHAL 'DEBS GNANG STE, 'GOS LO TZ'A BA GZHON NU DPAL GYIS MDZAD
PA'I DEB

THER SNGON PO 'DI NYID DEB GRANGS GCIG STONG THAM PA PAR BSKRUN
GNANG BA DANG, DE'I

SKABS DPE CHA ZHU BSGRIGS KYI 'GAN 'KHUR BA KARMA BLO GROS 'BYOR
LDAN NAM TSE RING

BCAS, THAMS CAD KYIS PHYAR BA GRU 'DEGS GNANG BA LA SNYING THAG
PA NAS THUGS RJE

CHE ZHES ZHU RGYU DANG, MA 'ONGS PAR PHYAG DPE GZIGS MKHAN RNAMS
KYIS DPE CHA

'DI'I STENG NAS SLOB SBYANG, ZHIB 'JUG, NYAMS LEN GANG GZAB KYIS
RANG DON DU

THOS BSAM SGOM GSUM, GZHAN DON DU 'CHAD RTZOD RTZOM GSUM, GNYIS
DON DU

MKHAS BTZUN BZANG GSUM STE DAM PA'I NGANG TSUL DGU YIS DON GNYIS
LHUN GYIS

GRUB PA ZHIG YONG BA'I SMON 'DUN DANG, DE LTA BU GNANG ROGS ZHES
KYANG ZHU BA LAGS,

DE BZHIN MA PHYI GSAL PO MA THOB PA DANG, ZHU DAG GNAD SMIN MA
SONG BA SOGS KYIS

LHAG CHAD DANG, NOR 'KHRUL BYUNG BA THAMS CAD MKHAS PA'I DBANG
PO RNAMS KYI DRUNG DU

BSHAGS SHING, NOR BCOS BKA' BSLAB KYANG LHUG POR STZOL GNANG
BKA' DRIN ZHU,

KHRA 'GU SPRUL MING PAS , @671

PHAG MO GRU PA'I GDAN RABS KYI SKABS,

DE LTAR BU SLOB BYON PA'I RIM PA CHE BA RNAMS NI PHYI NAS 'CHAD
CING,

RAGS PA CIG BRJOD NAS GDAN SA'I TSUL LUGS NI, 'JAG SPYIL NA
BZHUGS

PA'I SKU 'DRA RIN PO CHE 'DI NI, GSHEGS RJES KHO NAR BU SLOB
RNAMS KYIS

SMAN DANG RIN PO CHE DANG DAR ZAB LA SOGS BSRES PA'I 'JIM PA LA
GDUNG

THAL MANG DU BTAB STE BZHENGS, BYIN RLABS KYANG SHIN TU CHE,
GSUNG

YANG LAN MANG DU BYON, BYI BAS SKU'I GDAN GYI ZUR NAS SA CUNG
ZAD BRUS

PA LA, DKON GNYER LA GSUNG BYON NAS BYI BAS GNOD PA BYAS PA'I
RJES

RNAMS BKAG SA DE RNAMS LA RU MA BYAS TE BZHENGS PA'I SKU
'DRA'ANG MANG

DU YOD PA LA, BYI SA MA ZHES GRAGS, BZO BYED PA'I TSE SKU'I CHA
SHAS NAS

LHAG PA RNAMS DRAS PA'I SA LA RU MA BYAS TE BZHENGS PA'I SKU
RNAMS LA NI DRAS

SA MA ZHES GRAGS, CHOS KHRI LA BZHUGS PA'I SKU 'DRA 'DI YANG MAR
PA LHA

SNYING BYA BAS MANG 'GAR SGANG DU BZHENGS, RAGS PA GRUB PA NA GA
NAS

'ONGS CHA MED PA'I JO MO MA CIG BYUNG NAS, NGA'I BLA MA DE 'DI
KHO NA 'DRA,

DA BCAS BCOS MA BYED ZER BAS NGO MTSAR DU GZUNG STE, CHOS KHRI'I

SU SPYAN DRANGS NAS BZHUGS SU GSOL BA YIN NO, ,DE NAS 'GRO MGON

GSHEGS RJES SU BLA MA ZHANG GIS DGE 'DUN GYI GRAL GONG DU BZHUGS
BSNGO BA

@672

TZAM MDZAD KYANG, LCAGS PHO STAG GI LO MJUG NAS ME PHO SPRE'U'I
BAR LO

BDUN DU GDAN SA BA MED, ME MO BYA NAS SA MO PHAG GI BAR LO NGO
GSUM

DU 'BRI KHUNG CHOS RJES GDAN SA MDZAD PA LA LONGS SPYOD KYANG
CHUNG ZHING MKHAN

PO BA LA SOGS PA'I GRVA PA RNAMS KYANG DAD PA CHUNG ZHING RE CHE
BAR BYUNG BAS,

'GRO MGON LA GSOL BA BTAB PA NA, 'GRO MGON BYON NAS ZA 'OG GI

'BOL RNYING PA ZHIG 'DUG PA 'DI KHONG RANG TSO LA GTONG LA,
KHYOD RANG DBU

RU BYANG PHYOGS SU SONG GSUNG BA'I LUNG BSTAN BYUNG BAS NAM
PHYED NA DPON

G-YOG LNGAS BROS BYON PAS, GNAS PO RDO BA'I SAR TSA BA LA PHEBS,
DES

ZHABS TOG BYAS SHING PHYAM TSE GSAR PA CIG KYANG PHUL, GSANG PHU
NAS LAM

BRGYUD NAS 'BRI KHUNG DU SA MO PHAG LA PHEBS SO, ,DE LTAR SA MO
PHAG GI

SMAD NAS ME MO YOS KYI BAR YANG GDAN SA PA MED, 'ON KYANG STAG
LUNG

CHOS RJES DGUNG LO LNGA BCU RTZA BDUN BZHES SHING, 'BRI KHUNG
CHOS RJES LNGA

BCU RTZA DRUG BZHES PA SA PHO RTA'I LO LA GTZUG LAG KHANG CHEN
MO BZHENGS TE,

DE YANG MANG 'GAR SGANG DU BZHENGS NA RDO RJE GDAN TSUN CHAD 'DU
BA CIG

'ONG BYAS NAS 'BRI KHUNG PAS GSUNGS PA LA, STAG LUNG BAS NGA'I
BLA MA'I

SKU RJEN PAR 'JOG PA MI 'ONG GSUNG NAS, GTZUG LAG KHANG GI NANG
DU

'JAG SPYIL YOD PA CIG BYED DGOS BYUNG BAS, RNAM PA GNYIS POS
BRAG RKON

CHEN MO MDZAD CING GTZUG LAG KHANG LEGS PAR BZHENGS, DER RTEN
DANG

GSUNG RAB KYANG MANG DU BYUNG, PHYI NAS NGAMS SHOD KYI BTZAD PO
GNYIS MA

@673

'CHAM PAS, BUD MED RNAMS GDAN SA BSHIG STE NGED RANG RNAMS KYI

CHOS RJES PHYAG RDZAS SHIN TU MANG BAR BSNAMS NAS BSAM YAS KYI

LA'ANG MANG DU BZHAG BTZAD PO GNYIS LA'ANG NOR MANG DU BYIN NAS

KYANG MA 'DUMS, 'ON KYANG MDZAD PA DES LO BCO BRGYAD KYI BAR DU

NI RTEN CING 'BREL BAR 'BYUNG BA DGONGS PAS, 'JIG RTEN PA DANG
MI

KHUNG PA

DANG STAG LUNG PA GNYIS KYIS BAR SKABS DER GDAN SA'I THUGS KHUR

BCUG CHOS RJE NYID THANG RKYANG MDZAD NAS PHYAG LEGS PAR MDZAD,

KHAMS PA GO CHA DANG, SLOB DPON PADMA'I DNGOS SLOB AA MI BYANG

RLANGS LHA GZIGS KYI RIGS TE, YAB YON CHEN RGYAL BA SKYABS DANG,

'BRO LDOG GZA' GYU GU LCAM GNYIS KYI SRAS SU SHING MO LUG LA

'DI PHAG MO GRU PA GSHEGS NAS LO DRUG PA YIN, DGUNG LO BCU GSUM
PA

LA SPYI GNAS G-YO GU ZHES BYA BAR MKHAN PO RDZONG MGO BA DANG,
SLOB DPON

STON PA ZHES PA THANG PO CHE BA GNYIS LA RAB TU BYUNG, MTSAN
GRAGS PA 'BYUNG

GNAS SU GSOL, RAB TU BYUNG NAS LO NGO GSUM DU BLA MA YE PHUG

SNGAR THUN 'JOG DANG LHAN CIG SKYES SBYOR LA SOGS PA'I KHRID
'GA' ZHUS,

DGUNG LO BCO LNGA PA LA YAB LA BLA MA YE PHUG PA'I PHYIR TAR DU

BYON,

DPON BLA MAS BSUN RTA DANG G-YOG CIG KYANG BTANG BYUNG, 'PHRAL

KHONG GIS GROGS MDZAD NAS MJAL DU BYON PAS CHOS RJE CHOS KHRI

BZHUGS PA DANG THOG MAR MJAL BAS, CHOS RJE ZHAL 'DZUM MDZAD NAS

PA YANG CHE, ZH'U'I GYON LUGS DANG BCAS PAS, KHYOD KYANG SGOM

PAR 'JOG CHOS RJE TSOGS SU 'BUL BA BZHES PA DANG, CHOS GSUNGS

BA SOGS PHRAN TSEGS THAMS CAD LA DUS MA YOL BAR MDZAD, RGYU

DES THAMS CAD LAS MNGON PAR 'PHAGS PAR GYUR PA YIN, CHOS RJES

SHOD KYI BTZAD PO DANG KHU SGOM SOGS CHE DGU RNAMS LA JA DANG

SBYIN BZANG PO MDZAD NAS, SLOB DPON 'DI GANGS TI SER BZHUD

'JIG RTEN NA 'GRAN ZLA MED PA CIG 'ONG BAS, KHYED NGAMS SHOD PA

'PHRAL DE LA, CHOS RJES LA RIL RGYAS BTAB PA CIG SKYEL BTANG

PA'I DBANG POS BSNGAGS PA'I 'DUL BA'I BCAS PA LAS MI NYAMS PA
DANG,

CHOS GSUNG BA'I TSE MA GTOGS SKU MTSAMS KHO NA LA BZHUGS, PHYI

KHA MCHU LA SOGS PA'I BYA BA MI MDZAD, DGE 'DUN RNAMS KYANG
THUGS DAM

LA BSKUL, MDZAD PA BLA NA MED PA DES NGAMS SHOD PA RNAMS KYANG
CHOS

RJE'I GSUNG KHO NA LTAR GDAN SA BRGYA 'GYUR STONG 'GYUR LA SONG,

RNAMS LA 'DI 'DRA BA'I BLA MA YOD ZER NAS MIG 'PHANGS MTHO BAR

BSAM YAS KYI LHA BTZUN ZHI BA 'OD KYI BU CIG NA NAS BRU SHA RIG
'DZIN PA

@678

LAM NAS BOS NAS RTZIS BYAS PAS, BU 'DI'I LO JO BO LA GNOD SKU
SROG

LA 'BAB ZER BAS, THABS MED DAM BYAS PAS, JO BO'I YUM LTO LA

BTANG NA DES THUB ZER NAS JO BO'I MA LTO LA BTANG BAS SHI, BUS
LO DRUG

LON BA'I TSE CI PHAN BYAS PAS DA LO CIS KYANG MI PHAN 'GRONGS
ZER, THABS

GTAN MED DAM BYAS PAS NGAMS SHOD KLUNGS NA BZANG BA'I DGE BSHES
SHIG LA

LTO THENGS NA THUB ZER, SU BZANG BYAS PAS RJE SPYAN SNGA BZANG
BAR KHA 'CHAM

NAS SPYAN DRANGS TE BSGYUR BAR BYAS PAS, BRU SHA NA RE, DE RTEN
'BREL

LA MNGA' BRNYES PA YIN PAR 'DUG PAS MI 'GYUR RAM ZER BAS MA NYAN
PAR,

CIS KYANG GDAN DRANGS NAS BSGYUR ZER NAS GDAN 'DREN BTANG BAS,
THAMS

CAD KYIS RJE SPYAN SNGA LA MI GSHEGS PAR ZHUS PAS, A'U RTZI
RKANG BZHI

THAMS CAD SENG GE GCIG GIS ZIL GYIS GNON PA DANG 'DRA, DAM BU
SENG

GE LTA BU'I RNAL 'BYOR PA YIN PAS GZHAN THAMS CAD ZIL GYIS GNON
PA YIN

GSUNG NAS THEGS, BRU SHAS DANG PO ZAM PA'I KHAR GROD PA CHUS
BLUG LA RI

MO SNA TSOGS BRIS NAS RLUNG GIS BSKYOD PA BYAS, ZAM PA'I KHAR
SPYANG KI'I

GZUGS LA GZUGS BRNYAN BSKYON, KHANG PA'I GONG LA LA YANG LTO
RIGS MANG

PO BYAS, BZHUGS KHRI 'OG NA YANG KHYI RO SKE BSNOL BA DANG, THOD

BYON PAS,

PA 'DUG ZER, SLOB DPON BRAM ZES RAG DUNG CIG KHUR YOD PA BUS

NAS BUS PAS, TZAG RGYANGS CAN CIG BYUNG BAS, DA DES CHOG GSUNG,

GSO BA LA GZUGS BRNYAN BSKYON PA DE KHO RANG LA KHA GTAD NAS

RJE'I ZHAL NAS, NYE GNAS KUN LA DANG POR KHRI DE GUL BA CIG
GYIS, DE

NAS LHUNG BZED DE ZHOG DES THUB GSUNG, ZHABS G-YON PA KHRI LA

LOG KHONG LA MI 'GYUR RAM BYAS PAS MA NYAN, DA NGA YANG YUL DU

BZHES, SNGAR DGON PA YUN RING DU RNYINGS PAS DGE 'DUN GYI NANG
NA HRAL

PHRAG BCU GNYIS GNAS PA NANG MA MTHUN PA LAS CIG GI PHYOGS BUD

SI'I DPUNG TSOGS

BSTAN PA GZHOM

G-YOS SHING

BZHI DPANG

SANGS RGYAS PA

LA

'JUG PA'I CHAD BYAS NAS THANG YANGS PAR SHING STAN BOR BAS CUNG
ZAD KYANG

LNGA PA'O,

KYIS G-YOGS TE

DER BLA MA BZHUGS SU BCUG PAS DONG DU LHUNG, KHA SHING DANG RDO
BA MANG

PO'I PHO

BRANG DU SPYAN DRONGS SHIG GSUNG PA LA RGYAL PO 'GYOD NAS ZHABS
SPYI BOS

BLANGS PA NI DRUG PA'O, SLAR RGYAL PO DE SHING SOG TU BCUG NAS
DE'I STENG

DU BLA MA BZHUGS TE ZHAG GSUM DU ME SBAR YANG MA TSIG PA NI BDUN
PA'O,
